first go through the calling process to
find publicly available web pages to add
to their innex this is like their way of
discovering and collecting information
from all over the Internet during The
Crawling process search engines boards
follow links from one page to another
discovering new content and updating
their index with the latest information
available on the web once the crawling
is done the search engine organizes
sorts and stores the information to find
it in the database which is called the
index this index is like a huge library
of web pages and it's what the search
engine uses to quickly find the right
information when someone searches for
something during The Crawling process
search engine boards also pay attention
to the instructions provided in the
robots.txt file which tells them which
page they are allowed to crawl and index

engine boards not to include that
particular page in their Index this

pages are made available to users

mechanisms help website owners manage
how their content is discovered and
indexed by search engines all right so
